add_namespace = france_md
add_namespace = France_news

# Invitation to French Alliance
country_event = {
	id = france_md.0
	title = france_md.0.t
	desc = france_md.0.d
	picture = GFX_french_flag_generic
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = france_md.0.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: france_md.0.o1 executed"
		FRA = {
			add_to_faction = ROOT
			country_event = diplomatic_response.1
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = france_md.0.o2
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: france_md.0.o2 executed"
		FRA = { country_event = diplomatic_response.2 }
		ai_chance = {
			base = 2.5
		}
	}

}

# European Investments
country_event = {
	id = france_md.1
	title = france_md.1.t
	desc = france_md.1.d
	picture = GFX_euro_investments
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = france_md.1.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: france_md.1.a executed"
		FRA = {
			country_event = france_md.2
			set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -10 }
			modify_treasury_effect = yes
			set_temp_variable = { int_investment_change = 10 }
			modify_international_investment_effect = yes
			set_country_flag = FRA_euro_investments_1
		}
		random_owned_state = {
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
			add_building_construction = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
			add_building_construction = {
				type = arms_factory
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 2 }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_index = FRA.id }
		change_influence_percentage = yes
		ai_chance = {
			base = 6
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = france_md.1.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: france_md.1.b executed"
		FRA = { country_event = france_md.3 }
		ai_chance = {
			base = 2
		}
	}

}

# [Root.GetName] accepts!
country_event = {
	id = france_md.2
	title = france_md.2.t
	desc = france_md.2.d
	picture = GFX_political_deal
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = france_md.2.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: france_md.2.a executed"
		if = { limit = { has_country_flag = FRA_euro_investments_1 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = FRA_euro_investments_cost_TT
			effect_tooltip = {
				set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -10 }
				modify_treasury_effect = yes
				set_temp_variable = { int_investment_change = 10 }
				modify_international_investment_effect = yes
				newline = yes
				set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 2 }
				set_temp_variable = { tag_index = FRA.id }
				set_temp_variable = { influence_target = FROM.id }
				change_influence_percentage = yes
			}
			clr_country_flag = FRA_euro_investments_1
		}
		else_if = { limit = { has_country_flag = FRA_europe_investments_2 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = FRA_euro_investments_cost_2_TT
			effect_tooltip = {
				set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -5 }
				modify_treasury_effect = yes
				set_temp_variable = { int_investment_change = 5 }
				modify_international_investment_effect = yes
				newline = yes
				set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 2 }
				set_temp_variable = { tag_index = FRA.id }
				set_temp_variable = { influence_target = FROM.id }
				change_influence_percentage = yes
			}
			clr_country_flag = FRA_europe_investments_2
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
		}
	}

}

# Investments in Eastern Europe
country_event = {
	id = france_md.4
	title = france_md.4.t
	desc = france_md.4.d
	picture = GFX_invetsments_in_eastern_europe
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = france_md.4.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: france_md.4.a executed"
		random_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				infrastructure < 5
			}
			add_building_construction = {
				type = infrastructure
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		FRA = {
			set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -5 }
			modify_treasury_effect = yes
			set_temp_variable = { int_investment_change = 5 }
			modify_international_investment_effect = yes
			country_event = france_md.2
			set_country_flag = FRA_europe_investments_2
		}
		set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 2 }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_index = FRA.id }
		change_influence_percentage = yes
		ai_chance = {
			base = 6
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = france_md.4.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: france_md.4.b executed"
		FRA = { country_event = france_md.3 }
		ai_chance = {
			base = 4
		}
	}

}

# The Paris Convention
country_event = {
	id = france_md.5
	title = france_md.5.t
	desc = france_md.5.d
	picture = GFX_paris_convention
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = france_md.5.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: france_md.5.a executed"
		FRA = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = supported_the_unification }
			country_event = france_md.6
		}
		add_political_power = 50
		set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 2 }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_index = FRA.id }
		change_influence_percentage = yes
		ai_chance = {
			base = 40
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = no
				factor = 60
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = france_md.5.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: france_md.5.b executed"
		FRA = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = fled_the_union }
			country_event = france_md.7
		}
		leaving_EU = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = news.4
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 60
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = no
				factor = 40
			}
		}
	}

}

# Restoration of the Bonapartes
country_event = {
	id = france_md.9
	title = france_md.9.t
	desc = france_md.9.d
	picture = GFX_bonaparte_restoration
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = france_md.9.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: france_md.9.a executed"
		set_country_flag = FRA_house_of_bonaparte_crowned
		set_country_flag = FRA_bonaparte_name_switch
		news_event = France_news.99
		set_cosmetic_tag = FRA_AUTH_S_NAP
		clr_country_flag = dynamic_flag
		add_popularity = { ideology = nationalist popularity = 0.15 }
		recalculate_party = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { rul_party_temp = 23 }
			set_temp_variable = { disable_elections = 1 }
			change_ruling_party_effect = yes
		}
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Jean-Christophe, Prince Napoléon"
			picture = "jean_christophe_bonaparte.dds"
			ideology = Monarchist
			traits = {
				nationalist_Monarchist
				likeable
				businessman
				smooth_talking_charmer
			}
		}
	}

}

# Armenia
country_event = {
	id = france_md.100
	title = france_md.100.t
	desc = france_md.100.d
	picture = GFX_armenia_france
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		original_tag = FRA
		country_exists = ARM
	}

	# Support Armenia Politically
	option = {
		name = france_md.100.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: france_md.100.a executed"
		set_country_flag = FRA_send_arm_political
		effect_tooltip = {
			ARM = { add_political_power = 250 }
			FRA = { add_political_power = -75 }
		}
		ARM = { country_event = { id = france_md.101 days = 5 } }
	}

	option = {
		name = france_md.100.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: france_md.100.b executed"
		set_country_flag = FRA_send_arm_financially
		effect_tooltip = {
			ARM = {
				set_temp_variable = { debt_change = debt }
				multiply_temp_variable = { debt_change = 0.25 }
				clamp_temp_variable = { var = debt_change max = 50 }
				modify_debt_effect = yes
			}
			FRA = {
				set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = debt_change }
				multiply_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -0.85 }
				modify_treasury_effect = yes
			}
		}
		ARM = { country_event = { id = france_md.101 days = 5 } }
	}

	option = {
		name = france_md.100.c
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: france_md.100.c executed"
		set_country_flag = FRA_send_arm_military
		effect_tooltip = {
			FRA = {
				send_equipment = {
					equipment = infantry_weapons_1
					amount = 1000
					target = ARM
				}
			}
		}
		ARM = { country_event = { id = france_md.101 days = 5 } }
	}
}

# Armenia's event
country_event = {
	id = france_md.101
	title = france_md.101.t
	desc = france_md.101.d
	picture = GFX_message_signing
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		original_tag = ARM
		country_exists = FRA
	}

	option = {
		name = france_md.101.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: france_md.101.a executed"
		if = { limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = FRA_send_arm_political } }
			ARM = { add_political_power = 250 }
			FRA = { add_political_power = -75 }
		}
		if = { limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = FRA_send_arm_financially } }
			ARM = {
				set_temp_variable = { debt_change = debt }
				multiply_temp_variable = { debt_change = 0.25 }
				clamp_temp_variable = { var = debt_change max = 50 }
				modify_debt_effect = yes
			}
			FRA = {
				set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = debt_change }
				multiply_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -0.85 }
				modify_treasury_effect = yes
			}
		}
		if = { limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = FRA_send_arm_military } }
			FRA = {
				send_equipment = {
					equipment = infantry_weapons_1
					amount = 1000
					target = ARM
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
		}
	}

}

# The First Ivorian Civil War
country_event = {
	id = france_md.102
	title = france_md.102.t
	desc = france_md.102.t
	picture = GFX_france_operation_liconre
	is_triggered_only = yes

	# Back Laurent Gbagbo
	option = {
		name = france_md.102.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: france_md.102.a executed"
		if = {
			limit = { CDI = { has_country_leader = { name = "Laurent Gbagbo" ruling_only = yes } } }
			add_relation_modifier = {
				target = CDI
				modifier = generic_increased_military_support
			}
		}
		else = {
			random_country_with_original_tag = {
				original_tag_to_check = CDI
				limit = {
					has_country_leader = { name = "Laurent Gbagbo" ruling_only = yes }
				}
				FRA = {
					add_relation_modifier = {
						target = PREV
						modifier = generic_increased_military_support
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = france_md.102.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: france_md.102.b executed"
		add_relation_modifier = {
			target = FNC
			modifier = generic_increased_military_support
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = france_md.102.c
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: france_md.102.c executed"
		trigger = {
			any_country_with_original_tag = {
				original_tag_to_check = CDI
				has_war_with = CDI
				NOT = { tag = FNC }
			}
		}
		random_country_with_original_tag = {
			original_tag_to_check = CDI
			limit = {
				has_war_with = CDI
				NOT = { has_country_leader = { name = "Laurent Gbagbo" ruling_only = yes } }
			}
			FRA = {
				add_relation_modifier = {
					target = PREV
					modifier = generic_increased_military_support
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

# Senegalese Civil War
country_event = {
	id = france_md.105
	title = france_md.105.t
	desc = france_md.105.d
	picture = GFX_french_troops_africa
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		country_exists = SEN
		SEN = {
			OR = {
				has_war_with = CSM
				has_civil_war = yes
			}
		}
	}

	# Support Senegal
	option = {
		name = france_md.105.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: france_md.105.a executed"
		add_relation_modifier = {
			target = SEN
			modifier = generic_increased_military_support
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = france_md.105.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: france_md.105.b executed"
		random_other_country = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = SEN
				NOT = { tag = SEN }
				has_war_with = SEN
			}
			FRA = {
				add_relation_modifier = {
					target = PREV
					modifier = generic_increased_military_support
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = france_md.105.c
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: france_md.105.c executed"
		trigger = {
			country_exists = SEN
			CSM = { has_war_with = SEN }
		}
		add_relation_modifier = {
			target = CSM
			modifier = generic_increased_military_support
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}
}

# Opération Sangaris
country_event = {
	id = france_md.106
	title = france_md.106.t
	desc = france_md.106.d
	picture = GFX_france_operation_sangaris
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		original_tag = FRA
	}

	# Support the CAR
	option = {
		name = france_md.106.a

# Takuba Task Force
country_event = {
	id = france_md.108
	title = france_md.108.t
	desc = france_md.108.d
	picture = GFX_french_troops_africa
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		original_tag = FRA
	}

	# Support the Malian Government
	option = {
		name = france_md.108.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: france_md.108.a executed"
		trigger = {
			country_exists = MAL
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_relation_modifier = {
						target = MAL
						modifier = generic_increased_military_support
					}
				}
			}
			add_relation_modifier = {
				target = MAL
				modifier = generic_increased_military_support
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_relation_modifier = {
					target = TUA
					modifier = generic_increased_military_support
				}
			}
			recall_volunteers_from = TUA
			remove_relation_modifier = {
				target = TUA
				modifier = generic_increased_military_support
			}
		}
		send_equipment = {
			equipment = infantry_weapons_1
			target = MAL
			amount = 500
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = france_md.108.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: france_md.108.b executed"
		trigger = {
			country_exists = TUA
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_relation_modifier = {
						target = TUA
						modifier = generic_increased_military_support
					}
				}
			}
			add_relation_modifier = {
				target = TUA
				modifier = generic_increased_military_support
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_relation_modifier = {
					target = MAL
					modifier = generic_increased_military_support
				}
			}
			recall_volunteers_from = MAL
			remove_relation_modifier = {
				target = MAL
				modifier = generic_increased_military_support
			}
		}
		send_equipment = {
			equipment = infantry_weapons_1
			target = TUA
			amount = 500
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = france_md.108.c
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: france_md.108.c executed"
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_relation_modifier = {
					target = MAL
					modifier = generic_increased_military_support
				}
			}
			recall_volunteers_from = MAL
			remove_relation_modifier = {
				target = MAL
				modifier = generic_increased_military_support
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_relation_modifier = {
					target = TUA
					modifier = generic_increased_military_support
				}
			}
			recall_volunteers_from = TUA
			remove_relation_modifier = {
				target = TUA
				modifier = generic_increased_military_support
			}
		}
		random_other_country = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = MAL
				has_cosmetic_tag = MAL_ANSAR_DINE
			}
			FRA = {
				add_relation_modifier = {
					target = PREV
					modifier = generic_increased_military_support
				}
				send_equipment = {
					equipment = infantry_weapons_1
					target = PREV
					amount = 500
				}
			}
		}

# Haitian Coup
country_event = {
	id = france_md.109
	title = france_md.109.t
	desc = france_md.109.d
	picture = GFX_france_special_forces
	is_triggered_only = yes

	# Instigate the Coup
	option = {
		name = france_md.109.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: france_md.109.a executed"
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = HAI_haitian_civil_war }
		}
		random_list = {
			60 = {
				# USA Supporting us makes this easier
				modifier = {
					factor = 2
					USA = { has_country_flag = USA_intervene_in_haiti }
				}
				HAI = {
					set_temp_variable = { rul_party_temp = 3 }
					change_ruling_party_effect = yes
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = democratic
						last_election = "2000.11.1"
						election_frequency = 60
						elections_allowed = yes
					}
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Boniface Alexandre"
						picture = "boniface_alexander.dds"
						ideology = socialism
						traits = {
							western_socialism
							lawyer
							judiciary
						}
					}
				}
			}
			40 = {
				HAI = {
					start_civil_war = {
						ideology = democratic
						size = 0.3
						states = { 859 }
					}
					hidden_effect = {
						set_temp_variable = { rul_party_temp = 13 }
						change_ruling_party_effect = yes
						set_politics = {
							ruling_party = neutrality
							last_election = "2000.11.1"
							election_frequency = 60
							elections_allowed = yes
						}
						create_country_leader = {
							name = "Buteur Métayer"
							picture = "buteur_metayer.dds"
							ideology = Neutral_Autocracy
							traits = {
								neutrality_Neutral_Autocracy
							}
						}
						FRA = {
							add_relation_modifier = {
								target = HAI
								modifier = generic_increased_military_support
							}
						}
						division_template = {
							name = "Rebel Forces"
							is_locked = yes
							regiments = {
								Militia_Bat = { x = 0 y = 0 }
								Militia_Bat = { x = 0 y = 1 }
								Militia_Bat = { x = 0 y = 2 }
								Militia_Bat = { x = 0 y = 3 }
							}
						}
						860 = {
							create_unit = {
								division = "name = \"1. Rebel Forces\" division_template = \"Rebel Forces\" start_experience_factor = 0.5 start_equipment_factor = 1"
								owner = HAI
							}
							create_unit = {
								division = "name = \"2. Rebel Forces\" division_template = \"Rebel Forces\" start_experience_factor = 0.5 start_equipment_factor = 1"
								owner = HAI
							}
						}
						random_other_country = {
							limit = {
								original_tag = HAI
								has_government = democratic
							}
							create_country_leader = {
								name = "Jean-Bertrand Aristide"
								picture = "jean-bertrand_artistide.dds"
								ideology = socialism
								traits = {
									western_socialism
									cleric
								}
							}
							division_template = {
								name = "Police Forces"
								is_locked = yes
								regiments = {
									Militia_Bat = { x = 0 y = 0 }
									Militia_Bat = { x = 0 y = 1 }
									Militia_Bat = { x = 0 y = 2 }
									Militia_Bat = { x = 0 y = 3 }
								}
							}
							859 = {
								create_unit = {
									division = "name = \"1. Police Forces\" division_template = \"Police Forces\" start_experience_factor = 0.5 start_equipment_factor = 1"
									owner = PREV
								}
								create_unit = {
									division = "name = \"2. Police Forces\" division_template = \"Police Forces\" start_experience_factor = 0.5 start_equipment_factor = 1"
									owner = PREV
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = france_md.109.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: france_md.109.b executed"
		trigger = {
			has_global_flag = HAI_haitian_civil_war
		}
		add_relation_modifier = {
			target = HAI
			modifier = generic_increased_military_support
		}
		send_equipment = {
			equipment = infantry_weapons_1
			target = HAI
			amount = 500
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
		}
	}

}

	id = france_md.110
	title = france_md.110.t
	desc = france_md.110.d
	picture = GFX_france_mayotte_referendum
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		original_tag = FRA
	}

	# Allow the Referendum
	option = {
		name = france_md.110.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: france_md.110.a executed"
		effect_tooltip = {
			activate_mission = COM_mayotte_referendum_mission
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = COM_mayotte_referendum_active
			COM = {
				set_country_flag = COM_mayotte_referendum_active
				# Current Expected Vote Share
				if = { limit = { NOT = { has_completed_focus = COM_anti_colonialist_propaganda } }
					set_variable = { COM.mayotte_referendum_france = 75 }
					set_variable = { COM.mayotte_referendum_comoros = 10 }
					set_variable = { COM.mayotte_referendum_independence = 15 }
				}
				else = {
					set_variable = { COM.mayotte_referendum_france = 60 }
					set_variable = { COM.mayotte_referendum_comoros = 25 }
					set_variable = { COM.mayotte_referendum_independence = 15 }
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = france_md.110.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: france_md.110.b executed"
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 20 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.04 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.04 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = france_md.110.c
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: france_md.110.c executed"
		set_country_flag = FRA_MTE_overseas_department
		release = MTE
		set_autonomy = {
			target = MTE
			autonomous_state = autonomy_french_overseas_department
			end_wars = no
			end_civil_wars = no
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}
}

			}
			561 = {

					instant_build = yes
				}

					type = fossil_powerplant
					level = 1

				}
			}
		}

country_event = {
	id = france_md.203
	title = france_md.203.t
	desc = france_md.203.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = france_md.203.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: france_md.203.a executed"
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { party_pop_array^18 > 0.6 } }
			country_event = { id = france_md.204 days = 10 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { party_pop_array^18 < 0.25 } }
			country_event = { id = france_md.205 days = 10 }
		}
		else = {
			random_list = {
				70 = {
					country_event = { id = france_md.204 days = 10 }

				}
				30 = {
					country_event = { id = france_md.205 days = 10 }
				}
			}
		}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
	}

	desc = france_md.283.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	#infantry

		name = france_md.283.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: france_md.283.a executed"
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = FRA_army_reformed_1 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = FRA_army_reformed_1
				add_idea = FRA_army_reformed_infantry
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
		}
	}

				add_idea = FRA_army_reformed_cavalry

			base = 1
		}
	}
}

country_event = {#surrounded by ennemy
	id = france_md.293
	title = france_md.293.t
	desc = france_md.293.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {#thanks
		name = france_md.293.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: france_md.293.a executed"
		add_war_support = 0.2
		add_stability = -0.1
		add_ideas = FRA_surrounded
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_in_faction_with = ENG
					original_tag = ENG
				}
			}
			FRA = {
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = FROM
					relation = military_access
					active = no
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = slightly_regulated_immigration }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = slightly_regulated_immigration
				add_idea = closed_borders
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = heavily_regulated_immigration }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = heavily_regulated_immigration
				add_idea = closed_borders
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = regulated_immigration }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = regulated_immigration
				add_idea = closed_borders
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_political_power = 150
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
		}
	}
}

country_event = {#alliance or war
	id = france_md.488
	title = france_md.488.t
	desc = france_md.488.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {#we join
		name = france_md.488.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: france_md.488.a executed"
		add_stability = 0.15
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 23 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.15 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.15 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		FRA= {
			if = {
					limit = { is_faction_leader = yes }
					FRA = { add_to_faction = ROOT }
			}
			else={
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = ROOT
					relation = guarantee
				}
				ROOT = {
					diplomatic_relation = {
						country = FRA
						relation = guarantee
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { temp_opinion = 5 }
		change_the_clergy_opinion = yes

		ai_chance = {
			base = 3
			modifier = {
				add = 1
				has_government = nationalist
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 1
				has_opinion = { target = FRA value > 50 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {#no
		name = france_md.488.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: france_md.488.b executed"
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 23 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = -0.05 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = -0.05 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		add_stability = -0.05
		FRA = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = FROM modifier = betrayed_our_cause }
			country_event = france_md.483
		}
		set_temp_variable = { temp_opinion = -5 }
		change_the_clergy_opinion = yes
		ai_chance = {
			base = 2
			modifier = {
				add = 2
				OR = {
					has_idea = great_power
					has_idea = large_power
					has_idea = super_power
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {#victory saint louis on europe
	id = france_md.489
	title = france_md.489.t
	desc = france_md.489.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {#convert europe
		name = france_md.489.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: france_md.489.a executed"
		add_stability = 0.2
		add_war_support = 0.1
		remove_ideas = FRA_expansion_crusades_plus
		add_ideas = FRA_victory_crusade_2_conversion
		every_other_country = {
			limit = { is_subject_of = FRA }
			if {
				limit={has_idea=pluralist}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = pluralist
					add_idea = christian
				}
				add_ideas = FRA_harsh_subjugation
			}
			if {
				limit={has_idea=orthodox_christian}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea =orthodox_christian
					add_idea = christian
				}
				add_ideas = FRA_harsh_subjugation
			}
			if {
				limit={has_idea=sunni}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea =sunni
					add_idea = christian

				}
				add_ideas = FRA_harsh_subjugation
			}
			if {
				limit={has_idea=shia}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea =shia
					add_idea = christian
				}
				add_ideas = FRA_harsh_subjugation
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 4
		}
	}
	option = {#they will see the light
		name = france_md.489.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: france_md.489.b executed"
		add_stability = 0.2
		add_war_support = 0.1
		remove_ideas = FRA_expansion_crusades
		add_ideas = FRA_victory_crusade_2_freedom_light
		every_other_country = {
			limit = { is_subject_of = FRA }
			add_ideas = FRA_enlightment
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 3
		}
	}
}

		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: france_md.497.a executed"
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 23 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.05 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.05 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		add_war_support = 0.15
		release_puppet = FROM
			set_autonomy = {
				target = FROM
				autonomy_state = autonomy_free
		}
		create_wargoal = {
			type = annex_everything
			target = FROM
		}
		FROM = {
			if = { limit = { is_in_faction = yes }
				leave_faction = yes
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 3
		}
	}
	option = {#nothing
		name = france_md.497.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: france_md.497.b executed"
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 23 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = -0.025}
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = -0.025}
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		release_puppet = FROM
			set_autonomy = {
				target = FROM
				autonomy_state = autonomy_free
		}
		FROM = {
			if = { limit = { is_in_faction = yes }
				leave_faction = yes
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -25
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
		}
	}

#build in eu

country_event = {#invest civ
	id = france_md.498
	title = france_md.498.t
	desc = france_md.498.d
	picture = GFX_united_states_dollar

	is_triggered_only = no

	option = {
		name = france_md.498.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: france_md.498.a executed"
		add_political_power = 25
		set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -4.50 }
		modify_treasury_effect = yes
		set_temp_variable = { int_investment_change = 4.5 }
		modify_international_investment_effect = yes
		set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 3 }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_index = FRA.id }
		set_temp_variable = { influence_target = THIS.id }
		change_influence_percentage = yes
		THIS = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = recently_invest
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				free_building_slots = {
					building = industrial_complex
					size > 0
					include_locked = yes
				}
				OR = {
					is_in_home_area = yes
					NOT = {
						owner = {
							any_owned_state = {
								free_building_slots = {
									building = industrial_complex
									size > 0
									include_locked = yes
								}
								is_in_home_area = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { modify_eurosceptic = 0.05 }
		set_temp_variable = { modify_eurosceptic_target = THIS }
		eurosceptic_change = yes
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 3 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.02 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		FRA = {
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = FRA_investing_eu
				days = 35
			}
			set_temp_variable = { int_investment_change = 4 }
			modify_international_investment_effect = yes
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 85
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = france_md.498.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: france_md.498.b executed"
		FRA = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = denied_us }
			country_event = diplomatic_response.2
			add_political_power = -25
			set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = 4 }
			modify_treasury_effect = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 15
		}
	}
}

# Liberal Arms Export Contracts
# france_md.323 - france_md.330

# France proposes arms contract to Saudi Arabia
country_event = {
	id = france_md.323
	title = france_md.323.t
	desc = france_md.323.d
	picture = GFX_message_signing
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		original_tag = FRA
		country_exists = SAU
		NOT = { has_war_with = SAU }
	}

	# Light weapons contract
	option = {
		name = france_md.323.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: france_md.323.a executed"
		set_country_flag = FRA_SAU_light_arms_contract
		effect_tooltip = {
			set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = 5 }
			modify_treasury_effect = yes
			SAU = {
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = infantry_weapons
					amount = 5000
				}
			}
		}
		SAU = { country_event = { id = france_md.324 days = 5 } }
		ai_chance = { base = 1 }
	}

	# Heavy weapons contract
	option = {
		name = france_md.323.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: france_md.323.b executed"
		set_country_flag = FRA_SAU_heavy_arms_contract
		effect_tooltip = {
			set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = 15 }
			modify_treasury_effect = yes
			SAU = {
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = MBT_Equipment
					amount = 100
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = IFV_Equipment
					amount = 200
				}
			}
		}
		SAU = { country_event = { id = france_md.324 days = 5 } }
		ai_chance = { base = 2 }
	}

	# Premium contract (aircraft)
	option = {
		name = france_md.323.c
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: france_md.323.c executed"
		set_country_flag = FRA_SAU_premium_arms_contract
		effect_tooltip = {
			set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = 30 }
			modify_treasury_effect = yes
			SAU = {
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = Jet_Multirole_Equipment
					amount = 24
				}
			}
		}
		SAU = { country_event = { id = france_md.324 days = 5 } }
		ai_chance = { base = 1 }
	}

	# Decline
	option = {
		name = france_md.323.e
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: france_md.323.e executed"
		add_political_power = 25
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
	}
}

# Saudi Arabia receives arms contract proposal
country_event = {
	id = france_md.324
	title = france_md.324.t
	desc = france_md.324.d
	picture = GFX_message_signing
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		original_tag = SAU
		country_exists = FRA
	}

	# Accept
	option = {
		name = france_md.324.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: france_md.324.a executed"
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = FRA_SAU_light_arms_contract } }
			FRA = {
				set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = 5 }
				modify_treasury_effect = yes
				clr_country_flag = FRA_SAU_light_arms_contract
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = infantry_weapons
				amount = 5000
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = FRA_SAU_heavy_arms_contract } }
			FRA = {
				set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = 15 }
				modify_treasury_effect = yes
				clr_country_flag = FRA_SAU_heavy_arms_contract
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = MBT_Equipment
				amount = 100
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = IFV_Equipment
				amount = 200
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = FRA_SAU_premium_arms_contract } }
			FRA = {
				set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = 30 }
				modify_treasury_effect = yes
				clr_country_flag = FRA_SAU_premium_arms_contract
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = Jet_Multirole_Equipment
				amount = 24
			}
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FRA
			modifier = FRA_arms_contract_opinion
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 10 }
	}

	# Decline
	option = {
		name = france_md.324.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: france_md.324.b executed"
		FRA = {
			clr_country_flag = FRA_SAU_light_arms_contract
			clr_country_flag = FRA_SAU_heavy_arms_contract
			clr_country_flag = FRA_SAU_premium_arms_contract
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 1 }
	}
}

	desc = france_md.327.d
	picture = GFX_message_signing
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		original_tag = FRA
		country_exists = SER
		NOT = { has_war_with = SER }
	}

	# Light weapons contract
	option = {
		name = france_md.327.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: france_md.327.a executed"
		set_country_flag = FRA_SER_light_arms_contract
		effect_tooltip = {
			set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = 3 }
			modify_treasury_effect = yes
			SER = {
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = infantry_weapons
					amount = 3000
				}
			}
		}
		SER = { country_event = { id = france_md.328 days = 5 } }
		ai_chance = { base = 1 }
	}

	# Heavy weapons contract
	option = {
		name = france_md.327.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: france_md.327.b executed"
		set_country_flag = FRA_SER_heavy_arms_contract
		effect_tooltip = {

					type = MBT_Equipment
					amount = 50
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = IFV_Equipment
					amount = 100
				}
			}
		}
		SER = { country_event = { id = france_md.328 days = 5 } }
		ai_chance = { base = 2 }
	}

	# Premium contract (aircraft)
	option = {
		name = france_md.327.c

# Serbia receives arms contract proposal
country_event = {
	id = france_md.328
	title = france_md.328.t
	desc = france_md.328.d
	picture = GFX_message_signing
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		original_tag = SER
		country_exists = FRA
	}

	# Accept
	option = {
		name = france_md.328.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: france_md.328.a executed"
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = FRA_SER_light_arms_contract } }
			FRA = {
				set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = 3 }
				modify_treasury_effect = yes
				clr_country_flag = FRA_SER_light_arms_contract
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = infantry_weapons
				amount = 3000
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = FRA_SER_heavy_arms_contract } }
			FRA = {
				set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = 8 }
				modify_treasury_effect = yes
				clr_country_flag = FRA_SER_heavy_arms_contract
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = MBT_Equipment
				amount = 50
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = IFV_Equipment
				amount = 100
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = FRA_SER_premium_arms_contract } }
			FRA = {
				set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = 15 }
				modify_treasury_effect = yes
				clr_country_flag = FRA_SER_premium_arms_contract
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = Jet_Multirole_Equipment
				amount = 12
			}
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FRA
			modifier = FRA_arms_contract_opinion
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 10 }
	}

	# Decline
	option = {
		name = france_md.328.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: france_md.328.b executed"
		FRA = {
			clr_country_flag = FRA_SER_light_arms_contract
			clr_country_flag = FRA_SER_heavy_arms_contract
			clr_country_flag = FRA_SER_premium_arms_contract
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 1 }
	}
}

###################################
# Joint Weapon Projects
# france_md.335 - france_md.338

# Germany receives Franco-German joint project proposal (FCAS/MGCS)
country_event = {
	id = france_md.335
	title = france_md.335.t
	desc = france_md.335.d
	picture = GFX_message_signing
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		original_tag = GER
		country_exists = FRA
	}

	# Accept the proposal
	option = {
		name = france_md.335.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: france_md.335.a executed"
		FRA = { set_country_flag = FRA_germany_accepted_joint_project }
		add_tech_bonus = {
			name = FRA_joint_project_germany
			bonus = 0.25
			uses = 2
			category = CAT_mbt
		}
		add_tech_bonus = {
			name = FRA_joint_project_germany
			bonus = 0.25
			uses = 2
			category = CAT_jet_fighter
		}
		add_ideas = GER_FCAS_MGCS_project
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FRA
			modifier = FRA_joint_project_opinion
		}
		FRA = { country_event = { id = france_md.336 days = 1 } }
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_opinion = { target = FRA value > 50 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_war = yes
			}
		}
	}

	# Decline the proposal
	option = {
		name = france_md.335.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: france_md.335.b executed"
		add_political_power = 25
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				has_war = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

			}
		}
	}

	desc = france_md.970.d
	picture = GFX_FRA_terror_aftermath

	trigger = {
		original_tag = FRA
		FRA_can_have_minor_attack = yes
		NOT = { has_country_flag = FRA_terror_level_1 }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 600
		# Stability factors
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.3
			has_stability < 0.20
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_war = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			FRA_on_extremist_path = yes
		}
		# Intelligence agency factors - strong intel delays attacks
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			FRA_has_strong_intelligence = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			FRA_has_weak_intelligence = yes
		}
		# Police budget factors - high spending delays attacks
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			FRA_has_high_police_budget = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.6
			FRA_has_low_police_budget = yes
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = { flag = FRA_recent_terror_attack days = 90 }
		set_country_flag = FRA_terror_level_1
		# Begin terror wave - 5 year window for escalated attacks
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = FRA_terror_wave_active } }
			set_country_flag = { flag = FRA_terror_wave_active days = 1825 }
		}
	}

	# Declare state of emergency
	option = {
		name = france_md.970.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: france_md.970.a executed"
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_war_support = 0.05
		add_political_power = -50
		add_manpower = -150
		add_ideas = FRA_state_of_emergency_terrorism
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = FRA_terror_threat_elevated
			days = 365
		}
		# Blocks further attacks temporarily
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = { flag = FRA_heightened_alert days = 180 }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 5 }
	}

	# Heighten security but maintain normal life
	option = {
		name = france_md.970.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: france_md.970.b executed"
		add_stability = -0.08
		add_war_support = 0.03
		add_political_power = -25
		add_manpower = -150
		add_ideas = FRA_heightened_security
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = FRA_terror_threat_elevated
			days = 365
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 3 }
	}

	# Minimal response (risky)
	option = {
		name = france_md.970.c
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: france_md.970.c executed"
		add_stability = -0.10
		add_war_support = 0.02
		add_manpower = -150
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = FRA_terror_threat_elevated
			days = 180
		}
		# More likely to have follow-up attack
		ai_chance = { base = 1 }
	}
}

# Level 2: Police Station or Recruitment Office Attack (Medium Attack)
country_event = {
	id = france_md.971
	title = france_md.971.t
	desc = france_md.971.d
	picture = GFX_FRA_police_station_attack

	trigger = {
		original_tag = FRA
		FRA_can_have_medium_attack = yes
		NOT = { has_country_flag = FRA_terror_level_2 }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 480
		# Stability factors
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.3
			has_stability < 0.20
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			NOT = { FRA_has_heightened_security = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			has_war = yes
		}
		# Intelligence agency factors
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.5
			FRA_has_strong_intelligence = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.4
			FRA_has_weak_intelligence = yes
		}
		# Police budget factors
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.8
			FRA_has_high_police_budget = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			FRA_has_low_police_budget = yes
		}
		# Terror wave acceleration - attacks breed more attacks
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_country_flag = FRA_terror_wave_active
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			has_country_flag = FRA_terror_level_1
		}
		# Terror wave can be broken by sustained security
		modifier = {
			factor = 5.0
			FRA_terror_wave_broken = yes
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = { flag = FRA_recent_terror_attack days = 120 }
		set_country_flag = FRA_terror_level_2
	}

	# Full military deployment to streets
	option = {
		name = france_md.971.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: france_md.971.a executed"
		add_stability = -0.08
		add_war_support = 0.08
		add_political_power = -75
		add_manpower = -50
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_idea = FRA_state_of_emergency_terrorism } }
			add_ideas = FRA_state_of_emergency_terrorism
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = FRA_terror_threat_elevated }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = FRA_terror_threat_elevated
				add_idea = FRA_terror_threat_critical
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_ideas = FRA_terror_threat_critical
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 5 }
	}

	# Intelligence-focused response
	option = {
		name = france_md.971.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: france_md.971.b executed"
		add_stability = -0.10
		add_war_support = 0.05
		add_political_power = -50
		add_manpower = -50
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = FRA_terror_threat_elevated }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = FRA_terror_threat_elevated
				add_idea = FRA_terror_threat_critical
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_ideas = FRA_terror_threat_critical
		}
		# Better chance to prevent next attack
		set_country_flag = { flag = FRA_intelligence_surge days = 365 }
		ai_chance = { base = 3 }
	}
}

		}

		add_war_support = 0.20

		add_manpower = -500

		air_experience = 25

				limit = { NOT = { tag = FRA } }

			}
		}

		}

			factor = 15.0
			FRA_has_strong_intelligence = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			FRA_has_weak_intelligence = yes
		}
		# Police budget factors
		modifier = {
			factor = 8.0
			FRA_has_high_police_budget = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			FRA_has_low_police_budget = yes
		}
		# Terror wave acceleration
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_country_flag = FRA_terror_wave_active
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			has_country_flag = FRA_terror_level_1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			has_country_flag = FRA_terror_level_2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			has_country_flag = FRA_terror_level_3
		}
		# Terror wave can be broken
		modifier = {
			factor = 5.0
			FRA_terror_wave_broken = yes
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = FRA_nuclear_threat
	}

	# Evacuate and neutralize threat
	option = {
		name = france_md.976.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: france_md.976.a executed"
		add_stability = -0.20
		add_war_support = 0.20
		add_political_power = -200
		add_manpower = -50

		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { id = france_md.983 days = 1 }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 5 }
	}

	# Special forces assault

		name = france_md.976.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: france_md.976.b executed"
		random_list = {
			70 = { # Success
				add_stability = -0.15
				add_war_support = 0.25
				add_political_power = 100
				custom_effect_tooltip = FRA_nuclear_threat_neutralized_tt
			}
			30 = { # Partial success with damage
				add_stability = -0.30
				add_war_support = 0.10
				add_political_power = -150
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = FRA_damaged_infrastructure

		}

			news_event = { id = france_md.983 days = 1 }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 3 }
	}
}

# Intelligence Foils Planned Attack
country_event = {
	id = france_md.985
	title = france_md.985.t
	desc = france_md.985.d
	picture = GFX_FRA_police_operation

	trigger = {
		original_tag = FRA
		OR = {
			has_idea = FRA_heightened_security
			has_idea = FRA_state_of_emergency_terrorism
			# Strong intelligence can foil attacks even without emergency measures
			AND = {
				FRA_has_strong_intelligence = yes
				FRA_has_high_police_budget = yes
			}
		}
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = FRA_intelligence_surge
			FRA_has_strong_intelligence = yes
		}
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = FRA_terror_level_1
			has_country_flag = FRA_terror_level_2
			has_country_flag = FRA_terror_level_3
		}
		NOT = { has_country_flag = FRA_terror_chain_complete }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = FRA_attack_foiled_recently }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 180
		# Emergency measures help
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_idea = FRA_state_of_emergency_terrorism
		}
		# Strong intelligence dramatically increases chance to foil plots
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			FRA_has_strong_intelligence = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			FRA_has_weak_intelligence = yes
		}
		# High police budget helps catch terrorists
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.4
			FRA_has_high_police_budget = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			FRA_has_low_police_budget = yes
		}
		# More operatives = better surveillance
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			num_of_operatives > 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			num_of_operatives > 8
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = { flag = FRA_attack_foiled_recently days = 365 }
	}

	# Publicize the success
	option = {
		name = france_md.985.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: france_md.985.a executed"
		add_stability = 0.05
		add_war_support = 0.03
		add_political_power = 50
		set_country_flag = { flag = FRA_attack_foiled days = 180 }
		ai_chance = { base = 4 }
	}

	# Keep it quiet for operational security
	option = {
		name = france_md.985.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: france_md.985.b executed"
		add_stability = 0.02
		add_political_power = 25
		set_country_flag = { flag = FRA_attack_foiled days = 365 }
		# Longer protection but less morale boost
		ai_chance = { base = 3 }
	}
}
